generate_spell_name_effect = {
	choose_spell_structure_and_build_spell_name_effect = yes
}

choose_spell_structure_and_build_spell_name_effect = {
	# Examples:
		# article						of / of the
		# of_article					of
		# of_the_article				of the
		# the_article					the
		# conjunction					and / and the
		# and_conjunction				and

		# adjective						Chronological
		# adverb						Chronologically
		# noun							Chronology
		# pluralNoun					Chronologies
		# possessiveNoun				Chronology's
		# inTransVerb					Chronologizing
		# transVerb						Chronologized

		# title							Waymaster
		# possessiveTitle				Waymaster's
		# titleFem						Waymother
		# possessiveTitleFem			Waymother's
		# titleMasc						Wayfather
		# possessiveTitleMasc			Wayfather's

		# name							Adam
		# pluralName					Adams
		# possessiveName				Adam's
		# possessivePronouns			her

	get_random_spell_type_term_effect = yes

assign_aspect_words_effect = {
	assign_single_aspect_word_effect = { TERM_NUMBER = spell_name_type TYPE = spellType }
	assign_single_aspect_word_effect = { TERM_NUMBER = spell_name_term_0 TYPE = $WORD_0_TYPE$ }
    assign_single_aspect_word_effect = { TERM_NUMBER = spell_name_term_1 TYPE = $WORD_1_TYPE$ }
    assign_single_aspect_word_effect = { TERM_NUMBER = spell_name_term_2 TYPE = $WORD_2_TYPE$ }
    assign_single_aspect_word_effect = { TERM_NUMBER = spell_name_term_3 TYPE = $WORD_3_TYPE$ }
    assign_single_aspect_word_effect = { TERM_NUMBER = spell_name_term_4 TYPE = $WORD_4_TYPE$ }
}

###############
# SPELL NAMES #
###############

assign_single_aspect_word_effect = {
	random_list = {
#####################
# Grammatical Terms #
#####################
		100 = {
			trigger = {  
				OR = {
					flag:$TYPE$ = flag:article
					flag:$TYPE$ = flag:of_article
				}
			}
			assign_spell_term_number = { WORD = spell_name_of_article TERM_NUMBER = $TERM_NUMBER$ }
		}
		100 = {
			trigger = {  
				OR = {
					flag:$TYPE$ = flag:article
					flag:$TYPE$ = flag:of_the_article
				}
			}
			assign_spell_term_number = { WORD = spell_name_of_the_article TERM_NUMBER = $TERM_NUMBER$ }
		}
		100 = {
			trigger = {  
				flag:$TYPE$ = flag:article
			}
			assign_spell_term_number = { WORD = spell_name_the_article TERM_NUMBER = $TERM_NUMBER$ }
		}
		100 = {
			trigger = {  
				OR = {
					flag:$TYPE$ = flag:and
					flag:$TYPE$ = flag:and_the
				}
			}
			assign_spell_term_number = { WORD = spell_name_and_the_article TERM_NUMBER = $TERM_NUMBER$ }
		}
		100 = {
			trigger = {  
				flag:$TYPE$ = flag:and
			}

assign_spell_term_number = {
    #if = {
        #limit = {
        #    always = $ALLOW$
        #}
        set_variable = {
            name = $TERM_NUMBER$
            value = flag:$WORD$
        }
   	#}
}

get_random_generic_magic_spell_term_effect = {
	random_list = {
		3 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:arcane } }
		3 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:magic } }
		3 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:sorcery } }
		3 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:occult } }
		3 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:powerful } }
		2 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:enchantment } }
		2 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:bewitching } }
		1 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:ensorcellment } }
		1 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:supernatural } }
		1 = { add_to_variable_list = { name = spell_name_components target = flag:sunder } }
	}
}
